15.30.075   Collection of moneys
   
15.30.080   Dedication required as condition to land annexation
   
15.30.085   Use for park purposes
§ 15.30.005  REQUIRED.
   As a condition of approval of a final plat of subdivision, or of a final
plat of a planned unit development, or on application for permit for mobile
home park, each subdivider or developer of a planned unit development or mobile
home park, will be required to dedicate land for school sites, to serve the
immediate and future needs of the residents of the development, or make a cash
contribution in lieu of actual land dedication, or a combination of both at the
option of the village with the recommendation of the boards of education of the
school districts affected, in accordance with the criteria and formula set
forth in §§
15.30.010 through
15.30.070.
(Prior Code, § 16.04.010)  (Ord. 261, § 1 (part), passed - -1974)
§ 15.30.010  CRITERIA FOR REQUIRING SCHOOL SITE DEDICATION.
   (A)   Requirement and population ratio.
      (1)   The ultimate number of students to be generated by a subdivision or
planned unit development or mobile home park shall bear directly upon the
amount of land required to be dedicated for school sites.
      (2)   The land dedication requirement shall be determined by obtaining
the ratio of estimated children to be served in each school classification over
the maximum recommended number of students to be served in each school
classification as stated herein, and then apply the ratio to the minimum
recommended number of acres of land deemed needed to have sufficient land for
school sites to serve the estimated increased children in each school
classification, and if cash contribution is elected, apply the number of
required acres of land against the fair market value of the land.
   (B)   School classification and size of school site. School classifications
and size of school sites within the village’s jurisdiction shall be determined
in accordance with the following criteria:
 
School Classification By Maximum Number of Students Minimum Number of Acres of
Grades                   for Each School            Land for Each School Site
                         Classification             Classification
Elementary schools,
grades kindergarten      400 students               15 acres
through 5 (K-5)
Junior high schools,     500 students               25 acres
Grades 6 through 8 (6-8)
Senior high schools,
Grades 9 through 12 (9-  1,000 students             80 acres
12)
 
   (C)   Comprehensive school plan. The comprehensive school plan and/or the
standards adopted by the affected school district shall be used as a guideline
in locating sites.
(Prior Code, § 16.04.020)  (Ord. 261, § 1(A), passed - -1974; Ord. VG06-412,
passed 8-28-2006)
§ 15.30.015  CRITERIA FOR REQUIRING A CONTRIBUTION IN LIEU OF A SCHOOL SITE.
   (A)   Where the development is small and the resulting site is too small to
be practical or when the available land is inappropriate for a school site, the
village, with the recommendation of the board of education of the school
districts affected, shall require the subdivider or developer to pay a cash
contribution in lieu of the land dedication required. The cash contributions in
lieu of school sites shall be held in trust by the village or other public body
designated by the village for use in the acquisition of land for a school site
to serve the immediate or future needs of children from that subdivision or
development or for the improvement to any existing school site which already
serves such needs, or for use in the acquisition of land for a school site or
for the improvement or construction of any existing school buildings or site
made necessary by the additional children from that subdivision or development
in the school district.
   (B)   The formula for determining the required cash contribution in lieu of
a land dedication shall be as follows: minimum number of acres of land for each
school site ÷ maximum number of students for each school classification X
estimated student population per dwelling unit X fair market value of improved
land = cash contribution. By way of example, the following is provided for
future reference.
(Prior Code, § 16.04.030)  (Ord. VG06-412, passed 8-28-2006)
§ 15.30.020  FAIR MARKET VALUE.
   (A)   The cash contributions in lieu of land shall be based on the “fair
market value” of the acres of land in the area improved as specified in this
section, that otherwise would have been dedicated as school sites.
   (B)   It has been determined that the present “fair market value” of the
improved land in and surrounding the village is $55,000 per acre, and the
figure shall be used in making any calculation in this chapter unless the
subdivider or developer files a written objection thereto. In the event of any
objection, the Village Council shall conduct or may direct the Village Planning
and Zoning Board to conduct a public hearing based upon statutory notice for
the purpose of receiving evidence concerning the “fair market value” of the
improved land.
   (C)   The Village Council shall determine the “fair market value” based upon
the evidence at the public hearing. The Village of Gardner, on its own motion
or at the request of an affected school district, may from time to time amend
this provision to provide for a different fair market value.
   (D)   Notwithstanding the foregoing, the fair market value of the improved
acre of land in and surrounding the Village of Gardner shall automatically
increase on January 1 of each year beginning on January 1, 2007 at a rate of 3%
per year.
(Prior Code, § 16.04.040)  (Ord. VG06-412, passed 8-28-2006)
§ 15.30.025  CRITERIA FOR REQUIRING DEDICATION AND A FEE.
   There will be situations in subdivisions, planned unit developments or
mobile home parks when a combination of land dedication and a contribution in
lieu of land are both necessary. These occasions will arise when:
   (A)   Only a portion of the land to be developed is proposed as the location
for a school site. That portion of the land within the subdivision, planned
unit development or mobile home park falling within the school location shall
be dedicated as a site as aforesaid, and a cash contribution in lieu thereof
shall be required for any additional land that would have been required to be
dedicated; and/or
   (B)   A major part of the school site has already been acquired and only a
small portion of land is needed from the development to complete the site. The
remaining portions shall be required by dedication, and a cash contribution in
lieu thereof shall be required.
(Prior Code, § 16.04.050)  (Ord. 261, (B)(2), passed - -1974)

   The following Table of Population Density is generally indicative of current
and short range projected trends in family size for new construction, and shall
be used in calculating the amount of required dedication of acres of land where
the cash contribution in lieu thereof unless a written objection is filed
thereto by the subdivider or developer:

(Prior Code, § 16.04.060)  (Ord. VG06-412, passed 8-28-2006)
§ 15.30.035  CONSTRUCTION OF UNITS.
   (A)   Except for detached single-family units it shall be presumed that the
subdivider or developer intends to construct units within the maximum school
age population density permitted by the ordinances of the village.
   (B)   On property zoned R-2 for the construction of single-family detached
units, it shall be presumed that 95% of the units shall contain three bedrooms
and 5% of the units shall contain four bedrooms.
   (C)   (1)   All fractions shall be rounded to the nearest unit.
      (2)   These presumptions may be overcome by the subdivider or developer
specifying the units to be constructed.
(Prior Code, § 16.04.070)  (Ord. 261, § 1(D), passed - -1974; Ord. 291, § 3,
passed - -1978)
§ 15.30.040  RESERVATION OF ADDITIONAL LAND.
   Where the comprehensive plan or the standards of the village call for a
larger amount for school sites in a particular subdivision or planned unit
development or mobile home park than the developer is required to dedicate, the
land needed beyond the developer’s contribution shall be reserved for
subsequent purchase by the village or other public body designed by the
village; provided, that the acquisition must be made within one year from the
date of approval of the final plat or the issuance of the conditional use
permit.
(Prior Code, § 16.04.080)  (Ord. 261, § 1(E), passed - -1974)
§ 15.30.045  COMBINING WITH ADJOINING DEVELOPMENTS.
   Where the subdivision, planned unit development or mobile home park is less
than 40 acres, a school site which is to be dedicated should, where possible,
be combined with dedications for adjoining developments in order to produce
usable school sites without the hardship on a particular developer.
(Prior Code, § 16.04.090)  (Ord. 261, § 1(F), passed - -1974)
§ 15.30.050  TOPOGRAPHY AND GRADING.
   The slope, topography and geology of the dedicated site as well as its
surroundings must be suitable for its intended purposes.
(Prior Code, § 16.04.100)  (Ord. 261, § 1(G), passed - -1974)
§ 15.30.055  IMPROVED SITES.
   (A)   All sites shall be improved with water, sewer and streets (including
enclosed drainage and curb and gutter), and have available to it utilities as
applicable to the location of the site, or acceptable provision made therefore.
   (B)   Sidewalks shall be excluded. In addition, school sites shall be fine
graded, provided with a minimum of four inches of topsoil, and seeded as part
of the required land improvements unless otherwise permitted by the Village
Council.
(Prior Code, § 16.04.110)  (Ord. 261, § 1(H), passed - -1974; Ord. VG06-412,
passed 8-28-2006)
§ 15.30.060  REAL ESTATE CONVEYANCE REQUIREMENTS.
   (A)   The subdivider or developer shall be responsible for conveying good,
merchantable title to such sites, and shall be responsible for payment of all
real estate taxes to the date of conveyance, including any agricultural roll
back taxes which might be extended or levied against the sites, for any tax
years or periods prior to the time of conveyance. After payment of the taxes,
evidence of the payment shall be furnished to the village and the grantee.
   (B)   The amount of any general real estate taxes for the year of conveyance
shall be pro-rated to the date of delivery of deed.
   (C)   The amount of the general real estate taxes shall be based on the
assessor’s latest known rate, value and equalizer, if any, for the land being
conveyed.
   (D)   The subdivider or developer shall furnish the village and the grantee
with a survey of the land to be conveyed.
   (E)   A commitment for title insurance issued by a company authorized to do
business in Illinois in the amount of the fair market value of the land shall
be required as evidence of clear title.
   (F)   If within 30 days of receipt of the commitment, the village or grantee
objects in writing to defects in the title, the subdivider or developer shall
have 30 additional days from the date of delivery of the written objections to
cure the defects.
   (G)   Conveyance shall occur only after or simultaneously with the passage
of an ordinance by the village in which it indicates that the property will be
accepted by the village for school purposes.
   (H)   All sites to be dedicated shall be conveyed to the school district
either by warranty to trustee’s deed, or such form of conveyance as the school
district shall require subject only to the following:
      (1)   Acts done or suffered by, or judgments against the school district,
its successors and assigns;
      (2)   General taxes for the year of conveyance, and subsequent years;
      (3)   Zoning and building laws and/or ordinances;
      (4)   Public and utility easements of record which are reasonably
acceptable to the village and school district;
      (5)   Conditions and covenants of record as contained only in plats of
subdivision approved by the village;
      (6)   Rights-of-way for drainage ditches, feeders, laterals and
underground tile, pipe or other conduit; and
      (7)   Other exceptions to title that village and school district shall
find acceptable.
   (I)   Each conveyance shall be accompanied by an appropriate affidavit of
title. All deeds of conveyance pursuant to this chapter shall be recorded, at
the subdivider or developer’s sole expense, in the office of the Recorder of
Deeds of Grundy County.
(Ord. VG06-412, passed 8-28-2006)
§ 15.30.065  TIME OF CONVEYANCE OR PAYMENT.
   (A)   Subdivider or developer shall convey to the respective school
districts the land required under this chapter within 30 days after any
subdivision plat or final plat of a planned unit development is recorded in the
office of the Recorder of Deeds of the county.
   (B)   All improvements shall be completed within such time as is required by
the village. A subdivider or developer shall make any cash contributions
required under this chapter upon the sale of a lot or upon the issuance of a
building permit, whichever occurs first.
   (C)   All moneys shall be paid to the Village Clerk of the village and shall
be held in an account designated to be used solely for the purpose of holding
the funds. A certified copy of the resolution establishing the amount of the
contribution shall be filed in the office of the County Recorder of Deeds and
the office of the Village Clerk of the village.
   (D)   The village shall divide all moneys so received among the respective
school districts by grades and shall make disbursements upon written request
made 90 days in advance to the respective school districts in accordance with
the formula set forth in this chapter.
(Prior Code, § 16.04.120)  (Ord. 261, (part), passed - -1974; Ord. 291, § 2
(part), passed - -1978)
§ 15.30.070  VILLAGE CLERK’S CERTIFICATE.
   Certification of the annexed plat shall be as follows:

(Prior Code, § 16.04.130)  (Ord. 261, (part), passed - -1974; Ord. 291, § 2
(part), passed - -1978)
§ 15.30.075  COLLECTION OF MONEYS.
   This village shall have the right to delegate the responsibility for
collecting moneys due under this chapter to other public bodies designated by
the village.
(Prior Code, § 16.04.140)  (Ord. 261, § 1(J), passed - -1974)
§ 15.30.080  DEDICATION REQUIRED AS CONDITION TO LAND ANNEXATION.
   The dedications of land or cash contributions in lieu thereof required in
this chapter shall also be required as a condition to the annexation of any
land to the village and provisions therefor shall be incorporated in any pre-
annexation agreement governing the land.
(Prior Code, § 16.04.150)  (Ord. 261, § 2, passed - -1974)
§ 15.30.085  USE FOR PARK PURPOSES.
   (A)   The village shall have the right to elect to use for park purposes
without charge on any land dedicated to the schools under this chapter upon
written notice to the school districts affected, provided, and during that
period of time, the lands are not then used for school purposes.
   (B)   School district may terminate the village’s right to use any parcel of
land for park purposes by giving the village six months written notice of the
school district’s intent to use the land for school purposes at that time.
   (C)   Upon electing to use the land, village shall furnish evidence of
public liability insurance covering the village and school district in an
amount equal to that carried by the school district.
(Prior Code, § 16.04.160)  (Ord. 261, § 3, passed - -1974)
CHAPTER 15.35:  PAYMENT OF SCHOOL FACILITIES IMPACT FEES
Section
   
15.35.005   General provisions
   
15.35.010   Amount of fees
   
15.35.015   Use of fees
   
15.35.020   Payment of fees
   
15.35.025   Annual report
   
15.35.030   Indemnification
   
15.35.035   Covenant not to sue
   
15.35.040   Reservation of powers
   
15.35.045   Miscellaneous; effective date
   
Appendix A: School Facilities Impact Fee (K–12)
§ 15.35.005  GENERAL PROVISIONS.
   It shall hereafter be the policy of the Gardner Village Council of the
Village of Gardner to require the payment of the school facilities impact fees
created herein as a condition of the annexation of residential territory to the
Village of Gardner. Therefore, unless otherwise authorized or directed by the
Gardner Village Council, the annexation of residential territory after the
effective date of this chapter shall be effected pursuant to an annexation
agreement requiring the payment of school facilities impact fees in substantial
accordance with the provisions set forth in
Appendix A below, to compensate the school districts from the development, as a
condition of the issuance of a residential building permit. This chapter shall
have no application to properties that are annexed to the Village of Gardner
for uses other than residential.
(R07-255, passed 1-22-2007)
§ 15.35.010  AMOUNT OF FEES.
   (A)   The impact fees required hereunder shall be consistent with the table
set forth in
Appendix A to this chapter. The fees shall increase 3% annually on January 1 of
each year, except that the Gardner Village Council reserves the right, by
motion, to reduce the annual increase or completely waive any annual increase
in the sole and unilateral discretion of the Gardner Village Council.
   (B)   As population density, age distribution and local conditions change
over the years, the impact fees reflected in division (B)(1) above shall remain
subject to periodic review and amendment if necessary.
   (C)   In the event the owner of property annexed to the village files a
written objection to the impact fees reflected in division (A) above, he or she
shall submit evidence to the village in support of the objection. The school
districts shall also be permitted to submit evidence in response to the
objection. The village may make any adjustments it deems necessary.
(R07-255, passed 1-22-2007)
§ 15.35.015  USE OF FEES.
   The impact fees paid to the affected school districts may be used in each
affected school district’s Operations and Maintenance Fund, Transportation Fund
or Education Fund for any purpose served by the funds.
(R07-255, passed 1-22-2007)
§ 15.35.020  PAYMENT OF FEES.
   The owner of property annexed to the village shall pay the required school
facilities impact fees directly to the school district designated by the
affected school districts. The school district designated to accept payment
shall issue a receipt for the payment which must be presented to the village
prior to the issuance of a building permit.
(R07-255, passed 1-22-2007)
§ 15.35.025  ANNUAL REPORT.
   The village shall require an annual report from each school district in
receipt of school facilities impact fees required by this chapter during the
previous fiscal year of the respective school districts. The report shall be
due within 25 business days of the first day of each calendar year, and shall
account for the receipt and expenditure of any impact fees for the previous
fiscal year.
(R07-255, passed 1-22-2007)
§ 15.35.030  INDEMNIFICATION.
   The school districts, individually and collectively, as a condition of
receiving the impact fees required hereunder, shall indemnify and hold the
Village of Gardner, harmless from and against any loss, claims and causes of
actions of every kind incurred by the village as a result, either directly or
indirectly, of the passage of this chapter, or the administration or
enforcement thereof, including any so incurred as a result of a lawsuit brought
or threatened by the school districts. However, the school districts shall not
be required to indemnify and hold harmless the Village of Gardner from any
loss, claims and causes of actions resulting out of the negligence of the
village. If the village is sued by any owner of property to be annexed as a
result, directly or indirectly, of the passage of this chapter, except as a
result of the negligence of the village, the village, may, at its option,
undertake the defense thereof but all costs and expenses of the defense,
including attorneys fees, shall be immediately reimbursed by the school
districts. Should the school districts improperly use the impact fees as
specified in this chapter, the village may sue the school districts and shall
be entitled to recover as part of the judgment therein, or any settlement
thereof, all costs and expenses, including attorneys fees, incurred by the
village.
(R07-255, passed 1-22-2007)
§ 15.35.035  COVENANT NOT TO SUE.
   The school districts covenant and agree, as a condition of receiving the
impact fees and in addition to the indemnification provided in this chapter,
not to sue the village for any claims arising, directly or indirectly, out of
the passage of this chapter, or the administration or enforcement thereof.
(R07-255, passed 1-22-2007)
§ 15.35.040  RESERVATION OF POWERS.
   Nothing herein shall be construed so as to limit, condition or impair the
exercise of powers conferred on the Village of Gardner to annex territory,
enter into annexation agreements, regulate the zoning, subdivision or
development of land, to levy or impose taxes and fees or to exercise other
municipal functions and powers. The establishment of policy herein shall not be
construed as a contract with any party. This chapter may not be enforced by
private action. This chapter is subject to amendment or repeal. The failure to
conform to the policy set forth herein shall not invalidate any official act of
the Village of Gardner, including, but not limited to, the annexation of
territory.
(R07-255, passed 1-22-2007)
§ 15.35.045  MISCELLANEOUS; EFFECTIVE DATE.
   (A)   If any term, condition or provision of this chapter shall be declared
unenforceable, the declaration of unenforceability shall have no bearing or
effect on the remaining parts thereof not so affected.
   (B)   This chapter shall take effect immediately from and following its
passage, approval and publication as required by law.
(R07-255, passed 1-22-2007)
